## Instruction

Please read the content from localhost:30137 and summarize the information, providing each person's available time slots. Analyze team members' calendar availability and automatically recommend one 2-hour weekly meeting slot. Send the schedule arrangement to meeting administrator [jjones@mcp.com](mailto:jjones@mcp.com). The email content should include the meeting time (in a format like "Monday 9:00 AM to 11:00 AM every week") and the names of all participants. You need to follow the content format in `format.md`.

```json arguments
{
	"function": "() => {\n  // Try to get the calendar data by looking for the availability information\n  const calendarData = {};\n  \n  // Look for time slots and days\n  const timeElements = document.querySelectorAll('[id*=\"time\"],
	 .time,
	 [class*=\"time\"]');\n  const dayElements = document.querySelectorAll('[id*=\"day\"],
	 .day,
	 [class*=\"day\"]');\n  \n  // Get the availability grid\n  const availabilityElements = document.querySelectorAll('[style*=\"background\"],
	 [class*=\"avail\"],
	 [id*=\"avail\"]');\n  \n  // Get any text that shows participant names or availability counts\n  const participantInfo = document.querySelectorAll('div,
	 span,
	 td').forEach(el => {\n    if (el.textContent && el.textContent.includes('/10')) {\n      console.log('Availability info:',
	 el.textContent);\n    }\n  });\n  \n  // Try to get the calendar table structure\n  const tables = document.querySelectorAll('table');\n  let calendarTable = null;\n  tables.forEach(table => {\n    if (table.rows && table.rows.length > 5) {\n      calendarTable = table;\n    }\n  });\n  \n  if (calendarTable) {\n    const rows = calendarTable.rows;\n    console.log('Calendar table found with',
	 rows.length,
	 'rows');\n    for (let i = 0; i < Math.min(rows.length,
	 10); i++) {\n      console.log('Row',
	 i,
	 ':',
	 rows[i].textContent);\n    }\n  }\n  \n  // Look for any JavaScript variables that might contain the schedule data\n  const scripts = document.querySelectorAll('script');\n  scripts.forEach(script => {\n    if (script.textContent && script.textContent.includes('avail')) {\n      console.log('Found availability script:',
	 script.textContent.substring(0,
	 200));\n    }\n  });\n  \n  return {\n    timeElements: timeElements.length,
	\n    dayElements: dayElements.length,
	\n    availabilityElements: availabilityElements.length,
	\n    tablesFound: tables.length,
	\n    calendarTableRows: calendarTable ? calendarTable.rows.length : 0\n  };\n}"
```

```json arguments
{
	"function": "() => {\n  // Analyze the availability data to find the best 2-hour consecutive slots\n  const participants = [\n    \"Assistant\",
	 \"jinghanz\",
	 \"junteng\",
	 \"Junxian\",
	 \"shiqi\",
	 \"Ting Wu\",
	 \n    \"Wei Liu\",
	 \"Weihao Zeng\",
	 \"YANG Cheng\",
	 \"zengweihao96@gmail.com\",
	 \"Á´•Èõ®ËΩ©\",
	 \"ÈªÑË£ïÊåØ\"\n  ];\n  \n  // Time slots start from 9:00 AM and go to 5:00 PM (8 hours = 32 15-minute slots per day)\n  // Days: Mon,
	 Tue,
	 Wed,
	 Thu,
	 Fri (5 days)\n  // Total slots: 160 (32 slots * 5 days)\n  \n  const timeSlots = [];\n  const days = ['Monday',
	 'Tuesday',
	 'Wednesday',
	 'Thursday',
	 'Friday'];\n  \n  // Generate time slots for each day\n  for (let day = 0; day < 5; day++) {\n    for (let hour = 9; hour < 17; hour++) {\n      for (let quarter = 0; quarter < 4; quarter++) {\n        const minutes = quarter * 15;\n        const timeString = `${hour}:${minutes.toString().padStart(2,
	 '0')}`;\n        const ampm = hour >= 12 ? 'PM' : 'AM';\n        const displayHour = hour > 12 ? hour - 12 : (hour === 0 ? 12 : hour);\n        const displayTime = `${displayHour}:${minutes.toString().padStart(2,
	 '0')} ${ampm}`;\n        \n        timeSlots.push({\n          day: days[day],
	\n          time: displayTime,
	\n          slotIndex: day * 32 + (hour - 9) * 4 + quarter\n        });\n      }\n    }\n  }\n  \n  // Get availability data from the page\n  const availabilityData = [];\n  if (window.AvailableAtSlot && window.TimeOfSlot) {\n    for (let i = 0; i < window.TimeOfSlot.length; i++) {\n      availabilityData.push({\n        slotIndex: i,
	\n        availableCount: window.AvailableAtSlot[i] ? window.AvailableAtSlot[i].length : 0,
	\n        availableIds: window.AvailableAtSlot[i] || []\n      });\n    }\n  }\n  \n  // Find best 2-hour consecutive slots (8 consecutive 15-minute slots)\n  const bestSlots = [];\n  for (let i = 0; i <= availabilityData.length - 8; i++) {\n    let totalAvailability = 0;\n    let minAvailability = 10;\n    let isConsecutive = true;\n    \n    // Check if 8 consecutive slots are all on the same day\n    const startDaySlot = i % 32;\n    if (startDaySlot > 24) { // Can't fit 2 hours before day ends\n      continue;\n    }\n    \n    for (let j = 0; j < 8; j++) {\n      if (i + j >= availabilityData.length) {\n        isConsecutive = false;\n        break;\n      }\n      const availability = availabilityData[i + j].availableCount;\n      totalAvailability += availability;\n      minAvailability = Math.min(minAvailability,
	 availability);\n    }\n    \n    if (isConsecutive) {\n      const dayIndex = Math.floor(i / 32);\n      const startSlotInDay = i % 32;\n      const startHour = 9 + Math.floor(startSlotInDay / 4);\n      const startMinute = (startSlotInDay % 4) * 15;\n      const endHour = startHour + 2;\n      \n      bestSlots.push({\n        startSlot: i,
	\n        day: days[dayIndex],
	\n        startTime: `${startHour > 12 ? startHour - 12 : startHour}:${startMinute.toString().padStart(2,
	 '0')} ${startHour >= 12 ? 'PM' : 'AM'}`,
	\n        endTime: `${endHour > 12 ? endHour - 12 : endHour}:${startMinute.toString().padStart(2,
	 '0')} ${endHour >= 12 ? 'PM' : 'AM'}`,
	\n        totalAvailability,
	\n        minAvailability,
	\n        avgAvailability: totalAvailability / 8\n      });\n    }\n  }\n  \n  // Sort by average availability (descending)\n  bestSlots.sort((a,
	 b) => b.avgAvailability - a.avgAvailability);\n  \n  return {\n    participants,
	\n    totalParticipants: participants.length,
	\n    activeParticipants: window.AvailableIDs ? window.AvailableIDs.length : 10,
	\n    totalSlots: availabilityData.length,
	\n    bestSlots: bestSlots.slice(0,
	 5),
	 // Top 5 best slots\n    sampleAvailability: availabilityData.slice(0,
	 10)\n  };\n}"
}
```
